## What's New in v2.0

[](#whats-new-in-v20)

### Intelligent Design System Generation

[](#intelligent-design-system-generation)

The flagship feature of v2.0 is the **Design System Generator** - an AI-powered reasoning engine that analyzes your project requirements and generates a complete, tailored design system in seconds.

```
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|  TARGET: Serenity Spa - RECOMMENDED DESIGN SYSTEM                                      |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                                        |
|  PATTERN: Hero-Centric + Social Proof                                                  |
|     Conversion: Emotion-driven with trust elements                                     |
|     CTA: Above fold, repeated after testimonials                                       |
|     Sections:                                                                          |
|       1. Hero                                                                          |
|       2. Services                                                                      |
|       3. Testimonials                                                                  |
|       4. Booking                                                                       |
|       5. Contact                                                                       |
|                                                                                        |
|  STYLE: Soft UI Evolution                                                              |
|     Keywords: Soft shadows, subtle depth, calming, premium feel, organic shapes        |
|     Best For: Wellness, beauty, lifestyle brands, premium services                     |
|     Performance: Excellent | Accessibility: WCAG AA                                    |
|                                                                                        |
|  COLORS:                                                                               |
|     Primary:    #E8B4B8 (Soft Pink)                                                    |
|     Secondary:  #A8D5BA (Sage Green)                                                   |
|     CTA:        #D4AF37 (Gold)                                                         |
|     Background: #FFF5F5 (Warm White)                                                   |
|     Text:       #2D3436 (Charcoal)                                                     |
|     Notes: Calming palette with gold accents for luxury feel                           |
|                                                                                        |
|  TYPOGRAPHY: Cormorant Garamond / Montserrat                                           |
|     Mood: Elegant, calming, sophisticated                                              |
|     Best For: Luxury brands, wellness, beauty, editorial                               |
|     Google Fonts: https://fonts.google.com/share?selection.family=...                  |
|                                                                                        |
|  KEY EFFECTS:                                                                          |
|     Soft shadows + Smooth transitions (200-300ms) + Gentle hover states                |
|                                                                                        |
|  AVOID (Anti-patterns):                                                                |
|     Bright neon colors + Harsh animations + Dark mode + AI purple/pink gradients       |
|                                                                                        |
|  PRE-DELIVERY CHECKLIST:                                                               |
|     [ ] No emojis as icons (use SVG: Heroicons/Lucide)                                 |
|     [ ] cursor-pointer on all clickable elements                                       |
|     [ ] Hover states with smooth transitions (150-300ms)                               |
|     [ ] Light mode: text contrast 4.5:1 minimum                                        |
|     [ ] Focus states visible for keyboard nav                                          |
|     [ ] prefers-reduced-motion respected                                               |
|     [ ] Responsive: 375px, 768px, 1024px, 1440px                                       |
|                                                                                        |
+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
```

### How Design System Generation Works

[](#how-design-system-generation-works)

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  1. USER REQUEST                                                │
│     "Build a landing page for my beauty spa"                    │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                              │
                              ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  2. MULTI-DOMAIN SEARCH (5 parallel searches)                   │
│     • Product type matching (161 categories)                    │
│     • Style recommendations (67 styles)                         │
│     • Color palette selection (161 palettes)                    │
│     • Landing page patterns (24 patterns)                       │
│     • Typography pairing (57 font combinations)                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                              │
                              ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  3. REASONING ENGINE                                            │
│     • Match product → UI category rules                         │
│     • Apply style priorities (BM25 ranking)                     │
│     • Filter anti-patterns for industry                         │
│     • Process decision rules (JSON conditions)                  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                              │
                              ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  4. COMPLETE DESIGN SYSTEM OUTPUT                               │
│     Pattern + Style + Colors + Typography + Effects             │
│     + Anti-patterns to avoid + Pre-delivery checklist           │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 161 Industry-Specific Reasoning Rules

[](#161-industry-specific-reasoning-rules)

The reasoning engine includes specialized rules for:

Category

Examples

**Tech & SaaS**

SaaS, Micro SaaS, B2B Service, Developer Tool / IDE, AI/Chatbot Platform, Cybersecurity Platform

**Finance**

Fintech/Crypto, Banking, Insurance, Personal Finance Tracker, Invoice & Billing Tool

**Healthcare**

Medical Clinic, Pharmacy, Dental, Veterinary, Mental Health, Medication Reminder

**E-commerce**

General, Luxury, Marketplace (P2P), Subscription Box, Food Delivery

**Services**

Beauty/Spa, Restaurant, Hotel, Legal, Home Services, Booking & Appointment

**Creative**

Portfolio, Agency, Photography, Gaming, Music Streaming, Photo/Video Editor

**Lifestyle**

Habit Tracker, Recipe & Cooking, Meditation, Weather, Diary, Mood Tracker

**Emerging Tech**

Web3/NFT, Spatial Computing, Quantum Computing, Autonomous Drone Fleet

Each rule includes:

-   **Recommended Pattern** - Landing page structure
-   **Style Priority** - Best matching UI styles
-   **Color Mood** - Industry-appropriate palettes
-   **Typography Mood** - Font personality matching
-   **Key Effects** - Animations and interactions
-   **Anti-Patterns** - What NOT to do (e.g., "AI purple/pink gradients" for banking)

## Features

[](#features)

-   **67 UI Styles** - Glassmorphism, Claymorphism, Minimalism, Brutalism, Neumorphism, Bento Grid, Dark Mode, AI-Native UI, and more
-   **161 Color Palettes** - Industry-specific palettes aligned 1:1 with the 161 product types
-   **57 Font Pairings** - Curated typography combinations with Google Fonts imports
-   **25 Chart Types** - Recommendations for dashboards and analytics
-   **15 Tech Stacks** - React, Next.js, Astro, Vue, Nuxt.js, Nuxt UI, Svelte, SwiftUI, React Native, Flutter, HTML+Tailwind, shadcn/ui, Jetpack Compose, Angular, Laravel
-   **99 UX Guidelines** - Best practices, anti-patterns, and accessibility rules
-   **161 Reasoning Rules** - Industry-specific design system generation (NEW in v2.0)

## Installation

[](#installation)

### Using Claude Marketplace (Claude Code)

[](#using-claude-marketplace-claude-code)

Install directly in Claude Code with two commands:

```
/plugin marketplace add nextlevelbuilder/ui-ux-pro-max-skill
/plugin install ui-ux-pro-max@ui-ux-pro-max-skill
```

### Using CLI (Recommended)

[](#using-cli-recommended)

# Install CLI globally
npm install -g uipro-cli

# Go to your project
cd /path/to/your/project

# Install for your AI assistant
uipro init --ai claude      # Claude Code
uipro init --ai cursor      # Cursor
uipro init --ai windsurf    # Windsurf
uipro init --ai antigravity # Antigravity
uipro init --ai copilot     # GitHub Copilot
uipro init --ai kiro        # Kiro
uipro init --ai codex       # Codex CLI
uipro init --ai qoder       # Qoder
uipro init --ai roocode     # Roo Code
uipro init --ai gemini      # Gemini CLI
uipro init --ai trae        # Trae
uipro init --ai opencode    # OpenCode
uipro init --ai continue    # Continue
uipro init --ai codebuddy   # CodeBuddy
uipro init --ai droid       # Droid (Factory)
uipro init --ai kilocode    # KiloCode
uipro init --ai warp        # Warp
uipro init --ai augment     # Augment
uipro init --ai all         # All assistants

### Global Install (Available for All Projects)

[](#global-install-available-for-all-projects)

uipro init --ai claude --global   # Install to ~/.claude/skills/
uipro init --ai cursor --global   # Install to ~/.cursor/skills/

### Other CLI Commands

[](#other-cli-commands)

uipro versions              # List available versions
uipro update                # Update to latest version
uipro init --offline        # Skip GitHub download, use bundled assets
uipro uninstall             # Remove skill (auto-detect platform)
uipro uninstall --ai claude # Remove specific platform
uipro uninstall --global    # Remove from global install

## Prerequisites

[](#prerequisites)

Python 3.x is required for the search script.

# Check if Python is installed
python3 --version

# macOS
brew install python3

# Ubuntu/Debian
sudo apt update && sudo apt install python3

# Windows
winget install Python.Python.3.12

## Usage

[](#usage)

### Skill Mode (Auto-activate)

[](#skill-mode-auto-activate)

**Supported:** Claude Code, Cursor, Windsurf, Antigravity, Codex CLI, Continue, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Qoder, CodeBuddy, Droid (Factory), KiloCode, Warp, Augment

The skill activates automatically when you request UI/UX work. Just chat naturally:

```
Build a landing page for my SaaS product
```

> **Trae**: Switch to **SOLO** mode first. The skill will activate for UI/UX requests.

### Workflow Mode (Slash Command)

[](#workflow-mode-slash-command)

**Supported:** Kiro, GitHub Copilot, Roo Code, KiloCode

Use the slash command to invoke the skill:

```
/ui-ux-pro-max Build a landing page for my SaaS product
```

### Example Prompts

[](#example-prompts)

```
Build a landing page for my SaaS product

Create a dashboard for healthcare analytics

Design a portfolio website with dark mode

Make a mobile app UI for e-commerce

Build a fintech banking app with dark theme
```

### How It Works

[](#how-it-works)

1.  **You ask** - Request any UI/UX task (build, design, create, implement, review, fix, improve)
2.  **Design System Generated** - The AI automatically generates a complete design system using the reasoning engine
3.  **Smart recommendations** - Based on your product type and requirements, it finds the best matching styles, colors, and typography
4.  **Code generation** - Implements the UI with proper colors, fonts, spacing, and best practices
5.  **Pre-delivery checks** - Validates against common UI/UX anti-patterns

### Supported Stacks

[](#supported-stacks)

The skill provides stack-specific guidelines for:

Category

Stacks

**Web (HTML)**

HTML + Tailwind (default)

**React Ecosystem**

React, Next.js, shadcn/ui

**Vue Ecosystem**

Vue, Nuxt.js, Nuxt UI

**Angular**

Angular

**PHP**

Laravel (Blade, Livewire, Inertia.js)

**Other Web**

Svelte, Astro

**iOS**

SwiftUI

**Android**

Jetpack Compose

**Cross-Platform**

React Native, Flutter

Just mention your preferred stack in the prompt, or let it default to HTML + Tailwind.

## Design System Command (Advanced)

[](#design-system-command-advanced)

For direct access to the design system generator:

> Note: If you installed via Continue, replace `.claude/skills/` with `.continue/skills/` in the commands below. For Droid (Factory), use `.factory/skills/`.

# Generate design system with ASCII output
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "beauty spa wellness" --design-system -p "Serenity Spa"

# Generate with Markdown output
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "fintech banking" --design-system -f markdown

# Domain-specific search
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "glassmorphism" --domain style
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "elegant serif" --domain typography
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "dashboard" --domain chart

# Stack-specific guidelines
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "form validation" --stack react
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "responsive layout" --stack html-tailwind

### Persist Design System (Master + Overrides Pattern)

[](#persist-design-system-master--overrides-pattern)

Save your design system to files for **hierarchical retrieval across sessions**:

# Generate and persist to design-system/MASTER.md
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "SaaS dashboard" --design-system --persist -p "MyApp"

# Also create a page-specific override file
python3 .claude/skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "SaaS dashboard" --design-system --persist -p "MyApp" --page "dashboard"

This creates a `design-system/` folder structure:

```
design-system/
├── MASTER.md           # Global Source of Truth (colors, typography, spacing, components)
└── pages/
    └── dashboard.md    # Page-specific overrides (only deviations from Master)
```

**How hierarchical retrieval works:**

1.  When building a specific page (e.g., "Checkout"), first check `design-system/pages/checkout.md`
2.  If the page file exists, its rules **override** the Master file
3.  If not, use `design-system/MASTER.md` exclusively

**Context-aware retrieval prompt:**

```
I am building the [Page Name] page. Please read design-system/MASTER.md.
Also check if design-system/pages/[page-name].md exists.
If the page file exists, prioritize its rules.
If not, use the Master rules exclusively.
Now, generate the code...
```

## Architecture & Contributing

[](#architecture--contributing)

### For Users

[](#for-users)

The codebase has been restructured to use a **template-based generation system**. All platform-specific files (`.cursor/`, `.windsurf/`, `.kiro/`, `.factory/`, etc.) are now generated dynamically by the CLI.

**Always use the CLI to install:**

npm install -g uipro-cli
uipro init --ai <platform\>

This ensures you get the latest templates and correct file structure for your AI assistant.

### For Contributors

[](#for-contributors)

If you want to contribute to this project:

# 1. Clone the repository
git clone https://github.com/nextlevelbuilder/ui-ux-pro-max-skill.git
cd ui-ux-pro-max-skill

# 2. Understand the structure
src/ui-ux-pro-max/           # Source of truth (data, scripts, templates)
cli/                         # CLI installer (generates files from templates)
.claude/                     # Local dev/test for Claude Code skill
.factory/                    # Local dev/test for Droid (Factory) skill

# 3. Make changes in src/ui-ux-pro-max/
# - data/\*.csv              → Database files
# - scripts/\*.py            → Search engine & design system
# - templates/              → Platform-specific templates

# 4. Sync to CLI and test locally
cp -r src/ui-ux-pro-max/data/\* cli/assets/data/
cp -r src/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/\* cli/assets/scripts/
cp -r src/ui-ux-pro-max/templates/\* cli/assets/templates/

# 5. Build and test CLI
cd cli && bun run build
node dist/index.js init --ai claude --offline  # Test in a temp folder

# 6. Create PR (never push directly to main)
git checkout -b feat/your-feature
git commit -m "feat: description"
git push -u origin feat/your-feature
gh pr create

See [CLAUDE.md](/nextlevelbuilder/ui-ux-pro-max-skill/blob/main/CLAUDE.md) for detailed development guidelines.

### 1. FRAMEWORK / LIBRARY

This is a **Next.js 15.5.9** application (using the **App Router**, `src/app` directory structure) with **React 19.2.1** and **TypeScript 5**.

**Key framework features in use:**
- **App Router** (`src/app/` directory) with file-based routing
- **React Server Components** (RSC) -- several pages are async server components
- **Next.js Middleware** (`src/middleware.ts`) for subdomain-based tenant routing
- **Next.js API Routes** (`src/app/api/proxy-image/route.ts`)
- **Server Actions** via `next/headers` for retrieving request headers in RSCs
- **Dynamic metadata** generation (`generateMetadata`)
- **Turbopack** for development (`next dev --turbopack -p 9002`)

---

### 4. STYLING APPROACH

**Primary: Tailwind CSS v3.4** with a comprehensive configuration.

Key details:
- **Styling framework:** Tailwind CSS with PostCSS
- **CSS-in-JS:** None (no styled-components or emotion)
- **Utility merging:** `clsx` + `tailwind-merge` via the `cn()` utility in `src/lib/utils.ts`
- **Dark mode:** Class-based (`darkMode: ['class']` in tailwind.config.ts)
- **CSS custom properties:** HSL variables defined in `globals.css` for theming (`--primary`, `--background`, etc.)
- **Custom fonts:** Inter (body), Playfair Display (headline), Montserrat (display), Poppins -- loaded via Google Fonts
- **shadcn/ui:** 36 Re-usable UI components in `src/components/ui/` (button, card, dialog, sheet, toast, etc.), configured via `components.json`
- **Icons:** `lucide-react` icon library (specified in `components.json`)
- **Animations:** Custom keyframes in tailwind config (accordion, marquee, float, progress, scan)

---

### 5. BUILD SYSTEM / PACKAGE MANAGER

- **Package manager:** npm (npm)
- **Build system:** Next.js built-in build (`next build`)
- **Dev server:** `next dev --turbopack -p 9002`
- **Scripts:**
  - `dev` -- Turbopack dev server on port 9002
  - `build` -- Production build
  - `start` -- Start production server
  - `lint` -- Next.js lint
  - `typecheck` -- TypeScript type checking
  - `genkit:dev` / `genkit:watch` -- Google GenKit AI flow development
  - `postinstall` -- `patch-package` for post-install patches

---

### 6. ROUTING SETUP

**Framework-level routing** (Next.js App Router, file-based):

- Pages are placed in `src/app/<route>/page.tsx`
- Dynamic routes use `[param]` directory names: `product/[id]`, `category/[slug]`, `admin/company/edit/[id]`
- Nested layouts: Root layout at `src/app/layout.tsx` wraps all pages
- **No custom route groups** or parallel routes detected

**Custom middleware** (`src/middleware.ts`):
- Extracts subdomain from the `host` header
- Sets `x-company-domain` header for downstream consumption
- This enables **multi-tenant routing** where different subdomains load different configurations
- Localhost fallback: defaults to `bavahomefoods` tenant

**Navigation structure:**
- Top nav bar (Header): Home, Wishlist, Cart, Company Orders, Admin (owner-only), Profile (user icon)
- Bottom nav bar (mobile): Home, Wishlist, Cart, Company Orders, Admin, History
- Footer: Links to Privacy Policy, Terms & Conditions, Shipping & Delivery, Cancellation & Refund
- Search: Client-side product search dropdown in header
- Cart/Wishlist/History/Profile/Address/Company Orders: Implemented as **sheet components** (slide-out panels) rather than separate pages

**No other routing library** -- all routing is Next.js native.

---

### 7. ADDITIONAL ARCHITECTURAL PATTERNS

**Multi-tenant / White-label Architecture:**
- Subdomain-based tenant resolution via middleware
- `src/config/tenant-config.ts` defines ~14+ tenant configurations with per-tenant: theme colors, fonts, text content, features flags, layout settings, SEO metadata, animation styles
- Tenants include: `tirumalasarees`, `sandhyacollections`, `ananthajewellers`, `skfashions`, etc.
- `ThemeProvider` dynamically applies CSS custom properties at runtime based on tenant config

**State Management:**
- **Zustand** with `persist` middleware for: cart (`use-cart.ts`), wishlist (`use-wishlist.ts`)
- **React Context** for: tenant configuration (`TenantContext.tsx`), cart (`CartContext.tsx`)
- **TanStack React Query** for server state caching (`QueryProvider.tsx`)
- **React `cache()`** for server-side data caching on company details

**Payment Integration:**
- **Cashfree** (`@cashfreepayments/cashfree-js`) in dependencies
- **Razorpay** hook (`use-razorpay.ts`) present, suggesting Razorpay integration is planned/partial

**API Layer:**
- Centralized `api-client.ts` wrapper with: automatic Bearer token injection, 401 token refresh flow with retry, configurable cache (ISR), query parameters
- Base URL: `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` or `http://127.0.0.1:8080/api/v1/manaBuy-services`

**AI Integration:**
- Google GenKit (`@genkit-ai/google-genai`, `@genkit-ai/next`) for AI-powered features
- `src/ai/` directory with GenKit flow definitions
- Recommendation server action in `src/app/actions.ts` (currently using mock data fallback)

**Testing:** No test files or test configuration found (no Jest, Vitest, or Playwright configs detected).

**Authentication:** Simple localStorage-based auth (tokens, roles) with `use-auth.ts` hook. Role system: `CUSTOMER`, `OWNER`, `ADMIN`. No dedicated login/signup page detected in the app routes.
</task_result>

<skill_content name="ui-ux-pro-max">
# Skill: ui-ux-pro-max

# UI/UX Pro Max - Design Intelligence

Comprehensive design guide for web and mobile applications. Contains 67 styles, 96 color palettes, 57 font pairings, 99 UX guidelines, and 25 chart types across 13 technology stacks. Searchable database with priority-based recommendations.

## When to Apply

Reference these guidelines when:
- Designing new UI components or pages
- Choosing color palettes and typography
- Reviewing code for UX issues
- Building landing pages or dashboards
- Implementing accessibility requirements

## Rule Categories by Priority

| Priority | Category | Impact | Domain |
|----------|----------|--------|--------|
| 1 | Accessibility | CRITICAL | `ux` |
| 2 | Touch & Interaction | CRITICAL | `ux` |
| 3 | Performance | HIGH | `ux` |
| 4 | Layout & Responsive | HIGH | `ux` |
| 5 | Typography & Color | MEDIUM | `typography`, `color` |
| 6 | Animation | MEDIUM | `ux` |
| 7 | Style Selection | MEDIUM | `style`, `product` |
| 8 | Charts & Data | LOW | `chart` |

## Quick Reference

### 1. Accessibility (CRITICAL)

- `color-contrast` - Minimum 4.5:1 ratio for normal text
- `focus-states` - Visible focus rings on interactive elements
- `alt-text` - Descriptive alt text for meaningful images
- `aria-labels` - aria-label for icon-only buttons
- `keyboard-nav` - Tab order matches visual order
- `form-labels` - Use label with for attribute

### 2. Touch & Interaction (CRITICAL)

- `touch-target-size` - Minimum 44x44px touch targets
- `hover-vs-tap` - Use click/tap for primary interactions
- `loading-buttons` - Disable button during async operations
- `error-feedback` - Clear error messages near problem
- `cursor-pointer` - Add cursor-pointer to clickable elements

### 3. Performance (HIGH)

- `image-optimization` - Use WebP, srcset, lazy loading
- `reduced-motion` - Check prefers-reduced-motion
- `content-jumping` - Reserve space for async content

### 4. Layout & Responsive (HIGH)

- `viewport-meta` - width=device-width initial-scale=1
- `readable-font-size` - Minimum 16px body text on mobile
- `horizontal-scroll` - Ensure content fits viewport width
- `z-index-management` - Define z-index scale (10, 20, 30, 50)

### 5. Typography & Color (MEDIUM)

- `line-height` - Use 1.5-1.75 for body text
- `line-length` - Limit to 65-75 characters per line
- `font-pairing` - Match heading/body font personalities

### 6. Animation (MEDIUM)

- `duration-timing` - Use 150-300ms for micro-interactions
- `transform-performance` - Use transform/opacity, not width/height
- `loading-states` - Skeleton screens or spinners

### 7. Style Selection (MEDIUM)

- `style-match` - Match style to product type
- `consistency` - Use same style across all pages
- `no-emoji-icons` - Use SVG icons, not emojis

### 8. Charts & Data (LOW)

- `chart-type` - Match chart type to data type
- `color-guidance` - Use accessible color palettes
- `data-table` - Provide table alternative for accessibility

## How to Use

Search specific domains using the CLI tool below.

---


## Prerequisites

Check if Python is installed:

```bash
python3 --version || python --version
```

If Python is not installed, install it based on user's OS:

**macOS:**
```bash
brew install python3
```

**Ubuntu/Debian:**
```bash
sudo apt update && sudo apt install python3
```

**Windows:**
```powershell
winget install Python.Python.3.12
```

---

## How to Use This Skill

When user requests UI/UX work (design, build, create, implement, review, fix, improve), follow this workflow:

### Step 1: Analyze User Requirements

Extract key information from user request:
- **Product type**: SaaS, e-commerce, portfolio, dashboard, landing page, etc.
- **Style keywords**: minimal, playful, professional, elegant, dark mode, etc.
- **Industry**: healthcare, fintech, gaming, education, etc.
- **Stack**: React, Vue, Next.js, or default to `html-tailwind`

### Step 2: Generate Design System (REQUIRED)

**Always start with `--design-system`** to get comprehensive recommendations with reasoning:

```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "<product_type> <industry> <keywords>" --design-system [-p "Project Name"]
```

This command:
1. Searches 5 domains in parallel (product, style, color, landing, typography)
2. Applies reasoning rules from `ui-reasoning.csv` to select best matches
3. Returns complete design system: pattern, style, colors, typography, effects
4. Includes anti-patterns to avoid

**Example:**
```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "beauty spa wellness service" --design-system -p "Serenity Spa"
```

### Step 2b: Persist Design System (Master + Overrides Pattern)

To save the design system for hierarchical retrieval across sessions, add `--persist`:

```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "<query>" --design-system --persist -p "Project Name"
```

This creates:
- `design-system/MASTER.md` — Global Source of Truth with all design rules
- `design-system/pages/` — Folder for page-specific overrides

**With page-specific override:**
```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "<query>" --design-system --persist -p "Project Name" --page "dashboard"
```

This also creates:
- `design-system/pages/dashboard.md` — Page-specific deviations from Master

**How hierarchical retrieval works:**
1. When building a specific page (e.g., "Checkout"), first check `design-system/pages/checkout.md`
2. If the page file exists, its rules **override** the Master file
3. If not, use `design-system/MASTER.md` exclusively

### Step 3: Supplement with Detailed Searches (as needed)

After getting the design system, use domain searches to get additional details:

```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "<keyword>" --domain <domain> [-n <max_results>]
```

**When to use detailed searches:**

| Need | Domain | Example |
|------|--------|---------|
| More style options | `style` | `--domain style "glassmorphism dark"` |
| Chart recommendations | `chart` | `--domain chart "real-time dashboard"` |
| UX best practices | `ux` | `--domain ux "animation accessibility"` |
| Alternative fonts | `typography` | `--domain typography "elegant luxury"` |
| Landing structure | `landing` | `--domain landing "hero social-proof"` |

### Step 4: Stack Guidelines (Default: html-tailwind)

Get implementation-specific best practices. If user doesn't specify a stack, **default to `html-tailwind`**.

```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "<keyword>" --stack html-tailwind
```

Available stacks: `html-tailwind`, `react`, `nextjs`, `vue`, `svelte`, `swiftui`, `react-native`, `flutter`, `shadcn`, `jetpack-compose`

---

## Search Reference

### Available Domains

| Domain | Use For | Example Keywords |
|--------|---------|------------------|
| `product` | Product type recommendations | SaaS, e-commerce, portfolio, healthcare, beauty, service |
| `style` | UI styles, colors, effects | glassmorphism, minimalism, dark mode, brutalism |
| `typography` | Font pairings, Google Fonts | elegant, playful, professional, modern |
| `color` | Color palettes by product type | saas, ecommerce, healthcare, beauty, fintech, service |
| `landing` | Page structure, CTA strategies | hero, hero-centric, testimonial, pricing, social-proof |
| `chart` | Chart types, library recommendations | trend, comparison, timeline, funnel, pie |
| `ux` | Best practices, anti-patterns | animation, accessibility, z-index, loading |
| `react` | React/Next.js performance | waterfall, bundle, suspense, memo, rerender, cache |
| `web` | Web interface guidelines | aria, focus, keyboard, semantic, virtualize |
| `prompt` | AI prompts, CSS keywords | (style name) |

### Available Stacks

| Stack | Focus |
|-------|-------|
| `html-tailwind` | Tailwind utilities, responsive, a11y (DEFAULT) |
| `react` | State, hooks, performance, patterns |
| `nextjs` | SSR, routing, images, API routes |
| `vue` | Composition API, Pinia, Vue Router |
| `svelte` | Runes, stores, SvelteKit |
| `swiftui` | Views, State, Navigation, Animation |
| `react-native` | Components, Navigation, Lists |
| `flutter` | Widgets, State, Layout, Theming |
| `shadcn` | shadcn/ui components, theming, forms, patterns |
| `jetpack-compose` | Composables, Modifiers, State Hoisting, Recomposition |

## Example Workflow

**User request:** "Làm landing page cho dịch vụ chăm sóc da chuyên nghiệp"

### Step 1: Analyze Requirements
- Product type: Beauty/Spa service
- Style keywords: elegant, professional, soft
- Industry: Beauty/Wellness
- Stack: html-tailwind (default)

### Step 2: Generate Design System (REQUIRED)

```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "beauty spa wellness service elegant" --design-system -p "Serenity Spa"
```

**Output:** Complete design system with pattern, style, colors, typography, effects, and anti-patterns.

### Step 3: Supplement with Detailed Searches (as needed)

```bash
# Get UX guidelines for animation and accessibility
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "animation accessibility" --domain ux

# Get alternative typography options if needed
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "elegant luxury serif" --domain typography
```

### Step 4: Stack Guidelines

```bash
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "layout responsive form" --stack html-tailwind
```

**Then:** Synthesize design system + detailed searches and implement the design.

---

## Output Formats

The `--design-system` flag supports two output formats:

```bash
# ASCII box (default) - best for terminal display
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "fintech crypto" --design-system

# Markdown - best for documentation
python3 skills/ui-ux-pro-max/scripts/search.py "fintech crypto" --design-system -f markdown
```

---

## Tips for Better Results

1. **Be specific with keywords** - "healthcare SaaS dashboard" > "app"
2. **Search multiple times** - Different keywords reveal different insights
3. **Combine domains** - Style + Typography + Color = Complete design system
4. **Always check UX** - Search "animation", "z-index", "accessibility" for common issues
5. **Use stack flag** - Get implementation-specific best practices
6. **Iterate** - If first search doesn't match, try different keywords

---

## Common Rules for Professional UI

These are frequently overlooked issues that make UI look unprofessional:

### Icons & Visual Elements

| Rule | Do | Don't |
|------|----|----- |
| **No emoji icons** | Use SVG icons (Heroicons, Lucide, Simple Icons) | Use emojis like 🎨 🚀 ⚙️ as UI icons |
| **Stable hover states** | Use color/opacity transitions on hover | Use scale transforms that shift layout |
| **Correct brand logos** | Research official SVG from Simple Icons | Guess or use incorrect logo paths |
| **Consistent icon sizing** | Use fixed viewBox (24x24) with w-6 h-6 | Mix different icon sizes randomly |

### Interaction & Cursor

| Rule | Do | Don't |
|------|----|----- |
| **Cursor pointer** | Add `cursor-pointer` to all clickable/hoverable cards | Leave default cursor on interactive elements |
| **Hover feedback** | Provide visual feedback (color, shadow, border) | No indication element is interactive |
| **Smooth transitions** | Use `transition-colors duration-200` | Instant state changes or too slow (>500ms) |

### Light/Dark Mode Contrast

| Rule | Do | Don't |
|------|----|----- |
| **Glass card light mode** | Use `bg-white/80` or higher opacity | Use `bg-white/10` (too transparent) |
| **Text contrast light** | Use `#0F172A` (slate-900) for text | Use `#94A3B8` (slate-400) for body text |
| **Muted text light** | Use `#475569` (slate-600) minimum | Use gray-400 or lighter |
| **Border visibility** | Use `border-gray-200` in light mode | Use `border-white/10` (invisible) |

### Layout & Spacing

| Rule | Do | Don't |
|------|----|----- |
| **Floating navbar** | Add `top-4 left-4 right-4` spacing | Stick navbar to `top-0 left-0 right-0` |
| **Content padding** | Account for fixed navbar height | Let content hide behind fixed elements |
| **Consistent max-width** | Use same `max-w-6xl` or `max-w-7xl` | Mix different container widths |

---

## Pre-Delivery Checklist

Before delivering UI code, verify these items:

### Visual Quality
- [ ] No emojis used as icons (use SVG instead)
- [ ] All icons from consistent icon set (Heroicons/Lucide)
- [ ] Brand logos are correct (verified from Simple Icons)
- [ ] Hover states don't cause layout shift
- [ ] Use theme colors directly (bg-primary) not var() wrapper

### Interaction
- [ ] All clickable elements have `cursor-pointer`
- [ ] Hover states provide clear visual feedback
- [ ] Transitions are smooth (150-300ms)
- [ ] Focus states visible for keyboard navigation

### Light/Dark Mode
- [ ] Light mode text has sufficient contrast (4.5:1 minimum)
- [ ] Glass/transparent elements visible in light mode
- [ ] Borders visible in both modes
- [ ] Test both modes before delivery

### Layout
- [ ] Floating elements have proper spacing from edges
- [ ] No content hidden behind fixed navbars
- [ ] Responsive at 375px, 768px, 1024px, 1440px
- [ ] No horizontal scroll on mobile

### Accessibility
- [ ] All images have alt text
- [ ] Form inputs have labels
- [ ] Color is not the only indicator
- [ ] `prefers-reduced-motion` respected

4: import Link from 'next/link';
5: import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
6: import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
7: import { Separator } from '@/components/ui/separator';
8: import {
9:   Minus,
10:   Plus,
11:   ShoppingCart,
12:   Trash2,
13:   Heart,
14:   Tag,
15:   ArrowRight,
16:   X,
17: } from 'lucide-react';
18: import { useCart } from '@/hooks/use-cart';
19: import { useWishlist } from '@/hooks/use-wishlist';
20: import { useToast } from '@/hooks/use-toast';
21: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils'; // Assuming cn utility exists
22: 
23: import { useTenant } from '@/components/providers/TenantContext';
24: import { CheckoutSheet } from '@/components/checkout/CheckoutSheet';
25: 
26: export default function CartPage() {
27:   const { cart, updateQuantity, removeFromCart, getCartTotal, companyDetails } = useCart();
28:   const { wishlist, toggleWishlist } = useWishlist();
29:   const { toast } = useToast();
30:   const { text } = useTenant();
31: 
32:   if (cart.length === 0) {
33:     return (
34:       <div className="container mx-auto px-4 py-16 flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-[60vh]">
35:         <div className="flex flex-col items-center text-center space-y-6 max-w-md animate-in fade-in zoom-in duration-500">
36:           <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-primary/10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mb-2">
37:             <ShoppingCart className="h-10 w-10 text-primary" />
38:           </div>
39:           <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold tracking-tight">Your cart is empty</h2>
40:           <p className="text-muted-foreground text-lg">
41:             Looks like you haven't added anything to your cart yet.
42:           </p>
43:           <Button asChild size="lg" className="rounded-full px-8 h-12 text-base shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl transition-all">
44:             <Link href="/">Start Shopping</Link>
45:           </Button>
46:         </div>
47:       </div>
48:     );
49:   }
50: 
51:   const subtotal = getCartTotal();
52:   const minOrder = Number(companyDetails?.minimumOrderCost || 0);
53:   const freeDeliveryThreshold = Number(companyDetails?.freeDeliveryCost || 0);
54:   const isFreeDelivery = freeDeliveryThreshold > 0 && subtotal >= freeDeliveryThreshold;
55:   const shipping = isFreeDelivery ? 0 : parseFloat(companyDetails?.deliveryCost || '0');
56:   const total = subtotal + shipping;
57: 
58:   return (
59:     <div className="min-h-screen bg-background py-12">
60:       <div className="container mx-auto px-4 max-w-6xl">
61: 
62:         {/* Page Header */}
63:         <div className="relative text-center mb-12 space-y-2">
64:           <Button
65:             variant="ghost"
66:             size="icon"
67:             asChild
68:             className="absolute left-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-full h-10 w-10 md:hidden"
69:           >
70:             <Link href="/">
71:               <X className="h-6 w-6" />
72:             </Link>
73:           </Button>
74:           <h1 className="text-4xl font-extrabold tracking-tight text-foreground sm:text-5xl">
75:             Shopping Cart
76:           </h1>
77:           <p className="text-lg text-muted-foreground">
78:             Review your items and proceed to checkout.
79:           </p>
80:         </div>
81: 
82:         <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-12 gap-8 items-start">
83: 
84:           {/* Cart Items List */}
85:           <div className="lg:col-span-8 space-y-6">
86:             <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-border/50 overflow-hidden">
87:               <ul className="divide-y divide-border">
88:                 {cart.map((item) => (
89:                   <li key={item.cartItemId} className="p-6 flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-6 items-start sm:items-center bg-card rounded-2xl border hover:shadow-md transition-shadow duration-200">
90:                     {/* Product Image */}
91:                     <div className="relative h-24 w-24 sm:h-28 sm:w-28 flex-shrink-0 overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border bg-secondary/30">
92:                       <Image
93:                         src={item.imageUrl}
94:                         alt={item.name}
95:                         fill
96:                         className="object-cover"
97:                         data-ai-hint={item.imageHint}
98:                       />
99:                     </div>
100: 
101:                     {/* Content */}
102:                     <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col w-full min-h-[7rem] justify-between">
103: 
104:                       {/* Top Row: Title + Variants | Price */}
105:                       <div className="flex justify-between items-start w-full">
106:                         <div className="space-y-2">
107:                           <Link href={`/product/${item.id}`} className="font-bold text-xl text-foreground hover:text-primary transition-colors line-clamp-1 block mr-4">
108:                             {item.name}
109:                           </Link>
110: 
111:                           <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 items-center">
112:                             {/* Variant Pills (Gray) */}
113:                             {Object.entries(item.selectedVariants || {}).map(([key, value]) => (
114:                               <span key={key} className="bg-secondary text-foreground px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium">
115:                                 {value}
116:                               </span>
117:                             ))}
118:                             {/* Size Colour Pills (Teal/Green) */}
119:                             {item.selectedSizeColours && item.selectedSizeColours.map((sc) => (
120:                               <span key={sc.id} className="bg-primary/10 text-emerald-700 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium border border-primary/20">
121:                                 + {sc.name}
122:                               </span>
123:                             ))}
124:                           </div>
125:                         </div>
126: 
127:                         <p className="font-extrabold text-xl tabular-nums whitespace-nowrap">
128:                           ₹{((item.price + (item.selectedSizeColours?.reduce((acc, sc) => acc + sc.price, 0) || 0)) * item.quantity).toFixed(2)}
129:                         </p>
130:                       </div>
131: 
132:                       {/* Bottom Row: Quantity | Actions */}
133:                       <div className="flex items-end justify-between mt-4">
134:                         {/* Quantity Selector - Styled Pill */}
135:                         <div className="flex items-center bg-secondary/30 rounded-xl border">
136:                           <Button
137:                             variant="ghost"
138:                             size="icon"
139:                             className="h-9 w-9 rounded-l-xl hover:bg-background hover:text-destructive hover:shadow-sm transition-all"
140:                             onClick={() => updateQuantity(item.cartItemId, Math.max(1, item.quantity - 1))}
141:                             disabled={item.quantity <= 1}
142:                           >
143:                             <Minus className="h-4 w-4" />
144:                           </Button>
145:                           <span className="w-8 text-center text-sm font-bold text-foreground">{item.quantity}</span>
146:                           <Button
147:                             variant="ghost"
148:                             size="icon"
149:                             className="h-9 w-9 rounded-r-xl hover:bg-background hover:text-primary hover:shadow-sm transition-all"
150:                             onClick={() => updateQuantity(item.cartItemId, item.quantity + 1)}
151:                           >
152:                             <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
153:                           </Button>
154:                         </div>
155: 
156:                         {/* Actions */}
157:                         <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
158:                           <Button
159:                             variant="ghost"
160:                             size="icon"
161:                             className={cn("rounded-full h-10 w-10 text-muted-foreground hover:text-red-500 hover:bg-red-50 transition-colors", wishlist.some(i => i.id === item.id) && "text-red-500 bg-red-50")}
162:                             onClick={() => toggleWishlist(item)}
163:                           >
164:                             <Heart className={cn("h-5 w-5", wishlist.some(i => i.id === item.id) && "fill-current")} />
165:                           </Button>
166:                           <Button
167:                             variant="ghost"
168:                             size="icon"
169:                             className="rounded-full h-10 w-10 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive hover:bg-destructive/10 transition-colors"
170:                             onClick={() => {
171:                               removeFromCart(item.cartItemId);
172:                               toast({ description: `${item.name} removed from cart.` });
173:                             }}
174:                           >
175:                             <Trash2 className="h-5 w-5" />
176:                           </Button>
177:                         </div>
178:                       </div>
179:                     </div>
180:                   </li>
181:                 ))}
182:               </ul>
183:             </div>
184:           </div>
185: 
186:           {/* Order Summary */}
187:           <div className="lg:col-span-4 space-y-6">
188:             <div className="bg-card p-6 sm:p-8 rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-border/50 sticky top-24">
189:               <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-6">Order Summary</h2>
190: 
191:               {/* Free Delivery Logic */}
192:               {(() => {
193:                 const minOrder = Number(companyDetails?.minimumOrderCost || 0);
194:                 const freeDeliveryThreshold = Number(companyDetails?.freeDeliveryCost || 0);
195:                 const isFreeDelivery = freeDeliveryThreshold > 0 && subtotal >= freeDeliveryThreshold;
196:                 const shipping = isFreeDelivery ? 0 : parseFloat(companyDetails?.deliveryCost || '0');
197:                 const total = subtotal + shipping;
198:                 const canCheckout = subtotal >= minOrder;
199:                 const amountForFreeDelivery = Math.max(0, freeDeliveryThreshold - subtotal);
200: 
201:                 return (
202:                   <>
203:                     {/* Free Delivery Nudge */}
204:                     {amountForFreeDelivery > 0 && freeDeliveryThreshold > 0 && (
205:                       <div className="mb-6 bg-primary/10 p-3 rounded-xl border border-primary/20 shadow-sm">
206:                         <p className="text-xs text-primary font-bold mb-2 flex items-center gap-2">
207:                           <span className="bg-primary/100 text-primary-foreground rounded-full p-0.5"><Plus className="w-3 h-3" /></span>
208:                           Add <span className="font-extrabold text-base">₹{amountForFreeDelivery.toFixed(0)}</span> more for free delivery
209:                         </p>
210:                         <div className="h-1.5 w-full bg-primary/20 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
211:                           <div
212:                             className="h-full bg-primary/100 rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
213:                             style={{ width: `${Math.min(100, (subtotal / freeDeliveryThreshold) * 100)}%` }}
214:                           />
215:                         </div>
216:                       </div>
217:                     )}
218: 
219:                     <div className="space-y-4 text-sm">
220:                       <div className="flex justify-between text-muted-foreground">
221:                         <span>Subtotal</span>
222:                         <span className="font-medium text-foreground">₹{subtotal.toFixed(2)}</span>
223:                       </div>
224:                       <div className="flex justify-between text-muted-foreground">
225:                         <span>Shipping</span>
226:                         <span className={cn(isFreeDelivery ? "text-green-600 font-medium" : "")}>
227:                           {isFreeDelivery ? "FREE" : `₹${shipping.toFixed(2)}`}
228:                         </span>
229:                       </div>
230: 
231:                       <Separator className="my-2" />
232: 
233:                       <div className="flex justify-between items-baseline">
234:                         <span className="text-base font-bold">Total</span>
235:                         <span className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">₹{total.toFixed(2)}</span>
236:                       </div>
237:                     </div>
238: 
239:                     {/* Coupon Section */}
240:                     <div className="mt-8 space-y-3">
241:                       <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-1">
242:                         <Tag className="w-4 h-4" />
243:                         <span>Apply Coupon</span>
244:                       </div>
245:                       <div className="flex gap-2">
246:                         <Input placeholder="Enter code" className="bg-background/50 h-10 border-dashed focus-visible:ring-primary/20" />
247:                         <Button variant="secondary" className="h-10 px-4 font-semibold">Apply</Button>
248:                       </div>
249:                     </div>
250: 
251:                     {!canCheckout && (
252:                       <p className="mt-4 text-xs text-destructive text-center font-medium bg-destructive/10 py-2 px-3 rounded-lg border border-destructive/20">
253:                         Minimum order amount is ₹{minOrder.toFixed(0)}
254:                       </p>
255:                     )}
256: 
257:                     {/* Checkout Button */}
258:                     <CheckoutSheet>
259:                       <Button
260:                         size="lg"
261:                         disabled={!canCheckout}
262:                         className={cn(
263:                           "w-full mt-4 h-12 text-base font-bold rounded-xl shadow-lg transition-all",

282:                     </div>
283:                   </>
284:                 );
285:               })()}

115: // Reviews are now fetched from product.reviews
116: const getReviewStats = (reviews: any[]) => {
117:   if (!reviews || reviews.length === 0) return { average: 0, count: 0, distribution: [] };
118:   const count = reviews.length;
119:   const average = reviews.reduce((acc, r) => acc + r.rating, 0) / count;
120:   const distribution = [5, 4, 3, 2, 1].map(star => ({
121:     star,
122:     percentage: (reviews.filter(r => Math.floor(r.rating) === star).length / count) * 100
123:   }));
124:   return { average, count, distribution };
125: };

237:           setSelectedPricingId(firstPricing.id);
238: 
239:           // Default to first ACTIVE style if available
240:           if (firstPricing.sizeColours && firstPricing.sizeColours.length > 0) {
241:             const firstActiveColour = firstPricing.sizeColours.find(sc => sc.sizeColourStatus !== 'OUTOFSTOCK' && sc.sizeColourStatus !== 'INACTIVE') || firstPricing.sizeColours[0];
242:             setSelectedSizeColourId(firstActiveColour.id);
243:           }
244:         }
245: 
246:         // Initialize colour
247:         if (foundProduct && foundProduct.colors && foundProduct.colors.length > 0) {
248:           setSelectedColourId(foundProduct.colors[0].id);
249:         }
250: 
251:         // Initialize legacy variants
252:         if (foundProduct?.variants) {
253:           const initialState: Record<string, string> = {};
254:           foundProduct.variants.forEach((variant) => {
255:             initialState[variant.name] = variant.options[0];
256:           });
257:           setSelectedVariants(initialState);
258:         }
259: 
260:         setLoading(false);
261:       }
262:     }
263: 
264:     loadProduct();
265: 
266:     return () => { isMounted = false; };
267:   }, [id, companyDetails]);
268: 
269: 
270:   if (loading) {
271:     return (
272:       <div className="container mx-auto px-4 py-8 h-[60vh] flex items-center justify-center">
273:         <Loader2 className="h-8 w-8 animate-spin text-primary" />
274:       </div>
275:     );
276:   }
277: 
278:   if (!product) {
279:     return (
280:       <div className="container mx-auto px-4 py-12 md:py-24">
281:         <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center space-y-6 max-w-lg mx-auto mb-24">
282:           <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-secondary/30 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mb-2 animate-in zoom-in duration-500">
283:             <div className="relative">
284:               <Search size={40} className="text-muted-foreground" />
285:               <div className="absolute -bottom-1 -right-1 bg-background rounded-full p-1">
286:                 <div className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full bg-destructive/80" />
287:               </div>
288:             </div>
289:           </div>
290: 
291:           <div className="space-y-2">
292:             <h1 className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-headline font-bold text-foreground">
293:               Product Not Found
294:             </h1>
295:             <p className="text-muted-foreground text-lg">
296:               We couldn't locate the product you're looking for. It might have been moved or doesn't exist.
297:             </p>
298:           </div>
299: 
300:           <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4 w-full sm:w-auto pt-4">
301:             <Button onClick={() => router.push('/')} size="lg" className="rounded-full px-8 gap-2">
302:               <ArrowLeft size={16} /> Back to Home
303:             </Button>
304:             <Button variant="outline" size="lg" onClick={() => router.back()} className="rounded-full px-8">
305:               Go Back
306:             </Button>
307:           </div>
308:         </div>
309: 
310:         <Separator className="mb-12" />
311: 
312:         <div className="space-y-8">
313:           <div className="text-center">
314:             <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">Explore Popular Items</h2>
315:             <p className="text-muted-foreground">You might find something else you love</p>
316:           </div>
317:           <Recommendations />
318:         </div>
319:       </div>
320:     );
321:   }
322: 
323:   // Derived state for current pricing option
324:   const currentPricingOption = product.pricing?.find(p => p.id === selectedPricingId) || (product.pricing?.[0]);
325:   // Using 'SizeColours' terminology
326:   // Note: SizeColours price usually adds ON TOP of the variant price.
327: 
328:   // Get sizeColours available for current pricing option
329:   const availableSizeColours = currentPricingOption?.sizeColours || [];
330: 
331:   // Local state for selected sizeColours
332:   // Local state for selected sizeColours (hoisted to top)
333: 
334:   // Calculate total price
335:   const basePrice = currentPricingOption ? currentPricingOption.price : product.price;
336:   const sizeColoursPrice = availableSizeColours
337:     .filter(sc => sc.id === selectedSizeColourId)
338:     .reduce((sum, sc) => sum + sc.price, 0);
339: 
340:   // Calculate Price Logic (Mirror ProductCard)
341:   // 1. Resolve base price for this variant
342:   let effectiveBasePrice = basePrice;
343:   let originalPrice = basePrice;
344:   let offerPercentage = 0;
345: 
346:   const offerPercent = product.productOffer ? parseFloat(product.productOffer.toString().replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '')) : 0;
347: 
348:   // Condition A: Percentage Offer exists (and variant price matches base product price)
349:   if (offerPercent > 0 && basePrice === product.price) {
350:     const discountAmount = (basePrice * offerPercent) / 100;
351:     effectiveBasePrice = Math.round(basePrice - discountAmount);
352:     offerPercentage = offerPercent;
353:   }
354:   // Condition B: Explicit Variant Discount
355:   else if (currentPricingOption && currentPricingOption.priceAfterDiscount && currentPricingOption.priceAfterDiscount > 0) {
356:     effectiveBasePrice = currentPricingOption.priceAfterDiscount;
357:     originalPrice = currentPricingOption.price;
358:     offerPercentage = Math.round(((originalPrice - effectiveBasePrice) / originalPrice) * 100);
359:   }
360:   // Condition C: Explicit Product Discount (fallback)
361:   else if (basePrice === product.price && product.priceAfterDiscount && product.priceAfterDiscount > 0) {
362:     effectiveBasePrice = product.priceAfterDiscount;
363:     originalPrice = product.price;
364:     offerPercentage = Math.round(((originalPrice - effectiveBasePrice) / originalPrice) * 100);
365:   }
366: 
367:   const finalPrice = effectiveBasePrice + sizeColoursPrice;
368:   const hasDiscount = effectiveBasePrice < originalPrice;
369: 
370:   const handleAddToCart = () => {
371:     // Construct the product to add to cart
372:     const variantInfo = { ...selectedVariants };
373:     if (currentPricingOption) {
374:       variantInfo['Quantity'] = currentPricingOption.quantity;
375:     }
376: 
377:     const sizeColourObjects = availableSizeColours.filter(sc => sc.id === selectedSizeColourId);
378: 
379:     // Resolve selected colour object
380:     const selectedColour = product.colors?.find(c => c.id === selectedColourId);
381:     const colourToAdd = selectedColour ? {
382:       id: selectedColour.id,
383:       name: selectedColour.name,
384:       image: selectedColour.image || ''
385:     } : undefined;
386: 
387:     // Safety check for out of stock selection
388:     const isOutOfStock = product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ||
389:       (currentPricingOption?.sizeStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK') ||
390:       (sizeColourObjects.some(sc => sc.sizeColourStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK')) ||
391:       (selectedColour?.colourStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK');
392: 
393:     if (isOutOfStock) {
394:       toast({
395:         title: "Out of Stock",
396:         description: "One of the selected options is currently unavailable.",
397:         variant: "destructive",
398:       });
399:       return;
400:     }
401: 
402:     addToCart(
403:       { ...product, price: effectiveBasePrice, productSizeId: selectedPricingId || undefined },
404:       variantInfo,
405:       sizeColourObjects,
406:       colourToAdd
407:     );
408:     setCartOpen(true);
409:   };
410: 
411:   const isWishlisted = isInWishlist(product.id);
412: 
413:   return (
414:     <div className="container mx-auto px-4 py-8">
415:       <div className="mb-6">
416:         <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => router.back()} className="text-muted-foreground group">
417:           <ArrowLeft className="h-5 w-5 mr-2 group-hover:-translate-x-1 transition-transform" />
418:           Back
419:         </Button>
420:       </div>
421:       <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-8 lg:gap-12">
422:         {/* Product Image Carousel */}
423:         <div className="relative aspect-[4/5] w-full rounded-3xl overflow-hidden bg-secondary/10 border border-border/50 shadow-sm md:aspect-auto md:h-[480px]">
424:           {(() => {
425:             // Collect all possible images
426:             const imagesList: string[] = [];
427: 
428:             // Helper to check if an image is a known dummy/placeholder
429:             const isDummyImage = (src: string) => {
430:               if (!src) return true;
431:               return src.includes('images.unsplash.com') && src.includes('w=800&q=80'); // Assuming your PlaceHolderImages have similar pattern
432:             };
433: 
434:             // 1. Prioritize selected Size-Colour image
435:             if (selectedSizeColourId) {
436:               const sc = availableSizeColours.find(sc => sc.id === selectedSizeColourId);
437:               if (sc && sc.productPics && sc.productPics.trim() !== "") imagesList.push(sc.productPics);
438:             }
439: 
440:             // 2. If colours exist, add selected colour image
441:             if (product.colors && product.colors.length > 0) {
442:               const selected = product.colors.find(c => c.id === selectedColourId);
443:               if (selected && selected.image && selected.image.trim() !== "" && !imagesList.includes(selected.image)) {
444:                 imagesList.push(selected.image);
445:               }
446:             }
447: 
448:             // We have real variant images
449:             const hasVariantImages = imagesList.length > 0;
450: 
451:             // 3. Add base product image(s) ONLY IF we don't have variant images OR the base image is not a dummy
452:             if (product.images && product.images.length > 0) {
453:               product.images.forEach(img => {
454:                 if (img && !imagesList.includes(img)) {
455:                   // If we already have variant images, try to skip dummy base images
456:                   if (!hasVariantImages || !isDummyImage(img)) {
457:                     imagesList.push(img);
458:                   }
459:                 }
460:               });
461:             } else if (product.productImage && !imagesList.includes(product.productImage)) {
462:               if (!hasVariantImages || !isDummyImage(product.productImage)) {
463:                 imagesList.push(product.productImage);
464:               }
465:             } else if (product.imageUrl && !imagesList.includes(product.imageUrl)) {
466:               // Many placeholders use standard imageUrls. If we have a variant image, we skip the base image if it looks like a dummy.
467:               // We will be aggressive here and just skip default base single image if variant images exist, as the user requested.
468:               if (!hasVariantImages) {
469:                 imagesList.push(product.imageUrl);
470:               }
471:             }
472: 
473:             // Fallback if empty (should only happen if literally nothing is selected and no product image exists)
474:             if (imagesList.length === 0) {
475:               imagesList.push(product.imageUrl || ''); // Give it at least something
476:             }
477: 
478:             return <ProductImageCarousel images={imagesList} alt={product.name} />
479:           })()}
480: 
481:           {(product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' || product.productStatus === 'INACTIVE') && (
482:             <div className="absolute inset-0 z-20 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/5 backdrop-blur-[2px]">
483:               <div className="relative overflow-hidden px-8 py-3 rounded-2xl bg-white/10 backdrop-blur-md border border-white/20 shadow-[0_8px_32px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)] transform rotate-[-5deg] animate-in zoom-in duration-500">
484:                 {/* Shimmer Effect */}
485:                 <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/20 to-transparent -translate-x-full animate-[shimmer_2s_infinite]" />
486:                 <span className={cn(
487:                   "relative z-10 text-xl font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] drop-shadow-sm",
488:                   product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ? "text-rose-500" : "text-slate-400"
489:                 )}>
490:                   {product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ? "Sold Out" : "Unavailable"}
491:                 </span>
492:               </div>
493:             </div>
494:           )}
495:         </div>
496: 
497:         {/* Product Details */}
498:         <div className="flex flex-col gap-6">
499:           <div>
500:             <div className="space-y-1.5">
501:               <span className={cn(
502:                 "text-[10px] font-black tracking-[0.2em] uppercase block mb-1",
503:                 tenant.id.toLowerCase().includes('anantha') ? "text-primary/60 font-display tracking-[0.3em]" : "text-primary/60"
504:               )}>
505:                 {companyDetails?.companyName || 'Digi Turu'}
506:               </span>
507:               <h1 className={cn(
508:                 "text-2xl md:text-5xl font-bold text-foreground leading-[1.15] tracking-tight",
509:                 tenant.id.toLowerCase().includes('anantha') ? "font-headline uppercase" : "font-headline"
510:               )}>
511:                 {product.name}
512:               </h1>
513:             </div>
514: 
515:             <div className="flex items-baseline gap-3 mt-4">
516:               <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground tracking-tight">
517:                 Rs. {(finalPrice).toFixed(2)}
518:               </h2>
519:               {hasDiscount && (
520:                 <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground/60 line-through decoration-destructive/30 decoration-1">
521:                   Rs. {(originalPrice + sizeColoursPrice).toFixed(2)}
522:                 </span>
523:               )}
524:               {hasDiscount && (
525:                 <span className="text-xs font-bold text-white bg-emerald-500 px-2 py-1 rounded-full shadow-sm animate-in zoom-in ml-2">
526:                   {offerPercentage}% OFF
527:                 </span>
528:               )}
529:               <div className="flex-1" />
530:               <Button
531:                 variant="outline"
532:                 size="icon"
533:                 className={cn("rounded-full h-10 w-10 transition-colors", isWishlisted && "text-red-500 bg-red-50 border-red-200")}
534:                 onClick={() => toggleWishlist(product)}
535:               >
536:                 <Heart className={cn("h-5 w-5", isWishlisted && "fill-current")} />
537:               </Button>
538:             </div>
539:             <p className="text-[11px] font-medium text-muted-foreground/60 mt-1.5 flex items-center gap-2">
540:               <Check className="w-3 h-3 text-emerald-500" />
541:               Taxes included. {companyDetails?.freeDeliveryCost && `Free shipping on orders over ${companyDetails.freeDeliveryCost}/-`}
542:             </p>
543: 
544:             {/* Rating simplified - Random Logic */}
545:             <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-3">
546:               <div className="flex items-center gap-1 text-primary">
547:                 {(() => {
548:                   const pid = Number(product.id) || product.id.toString().charCodeAt(0);
549:                   const randomRating = 4.1 + (pid % 6) * 0.1;
550:                   return [...Array(5)].map((_, i) => (
551:                     <Star key={i} className={cn("h-4 w-4", i < Math.floor(randomRating) ? 'fill-primary text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground/30 fill-muted-foreground/30')} />
552:                   ));
553:                 })()}
554:               </div>
555:               <span className="text-muted-foreground text-sm font-medium ml-1">
556:                 ({(() => {
557:                   const pid = Number(product.id) || product.id.toString().charCodeAt(0);
558:                   return (4.1 + (pid % 6) * 0.1).toFixed(1);
559:                 })()})
560:               </span>
561:             </div>
562: 
563:             <p className="mt-4 text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed text-base">{product.description}</p>
564:           </div>
565: 
566:           {/* Metadata Grid (only if data exists) */}
567:           {(product.ingredients || product.bestBefore) && (
568:             <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 py-4 border-y border-border/50">
569:               {product.ingredients && (
570:                 <div className="space-y-1">
571:                   <span className="text-xs font-bold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">Ingredients</span>
572:                   <p className="text-sm font-medium">{product.ingredients}</p>
573:                 </div>
574:               )}
575:               {product.bestBefore && (
576:                 <div className="space-y-1">
577:                   <span className="text-xs font-bold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">Shelf Life</span>
578:                   <p className="text-sm font-medium">{product.bestBefore}</p>
579:                 </div>
580:               )}
581:             </div>
582:           )}
583: 
584:           {product.instructions && (
585:             <div className="bg-secondary/20 rounded-xl p-4 border border-border/50">
586:               <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{product.instructions}</p>
587:             </div>
588:           )}
589: 
590:           <div className="space-y-8">
591:             {/* Pricing Options (Select Quantity) */}
592:             {product.pricing && product.pricing.length > 0 && (
593:               <div className="space-y-4">
594:                 <div className="flex items-center justify-between pb-2 border-b border-border/30 mb-4">
595:                   <label className="text-xs font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-[0.15em]">Select Option</label>
596:                   <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-primary/60 bg-primary/5 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-primary/10">REQUIRED</span>
597:                 </div>
598:                 <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
599:                   {(() => {
600:                     const prices = product.pricing.map(p => p.price);
601:                     const allPricesSame = prices.every(p => p === prices[0]);
602: 
603:                     return product.pricing.map((option) => {
604:                       const isActive = option.sizeStatus !== 'INACTIVE' && option.sizeStatus !== 'OUTOFSTOCK';
605:                       const isSelected = selectedPricingId === option.id;
606: 
607:                       return (
608:                         <button
609:                           key={option.id}
610:                           onClick={() => {
611:                             if (!isActive) return;
612:                             setSelectedPricingId(option.id);
613:                             // Auto-select first ACTIVE style (not OOS) when size is changed
614:                             if (option.sizeColours && option.sizeColours.length > 0) {
615:                               const firstActiveColour = option.sizeColours.find(sc => sc.sizeColourStatus !== 'OUTOFSTOCK' && sc.sizeColourStatus !== 'INACTIVE') || option.sizeColours[0];
616:                               setSelectedSizeColourId(firstActiveColour.id);
617:                             } else {
618:                               setSelectedSizeColourId(null);
619:                             }
620:                           }}
621:                           className={cn(
622:                             "relative flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-1.5 px-3 rounded-xl border transition-all duration-300 h-11",
623:                             isSelected && isActive
624:                               ? "border-primary bg-primary/[0.03] shadow-sm scale-[1.02]"
625:                               : isActive
626:                                 ? "border-border/60 bg-background/50 hover:border-primary/20 hover:bg-background"
627:                                 : "cursor-not-allowed bg-muted/10 border-border/40 opacity-50"
628:                           )}
629:                         >
630:                           {!isActive && (
631:                             <div className="absolute inset-0 z-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/5 rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
632:                               <div className="relative overflow-hidden px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-white/20 backdrop-blur-md border border-white/20 shadow-sm rotate-[-4deg]">
633:                                 <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/10 to-transparent -translate-x-full animate-[shimmer_2s_infinite]" />
634:                                 <span className="relative z-10 text-[8px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider text-rose-500 drop-shadow-sm">
635:                                   Sold Out
636:                                 </span>
637:                               </div>
638:                             </div>
639:                           )}
640:                           {isSelected && isActive && (
641:                             <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 text-primary">
642:                               <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor"><path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth="2" d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" /></svg>
643:                             </div>
644:                           )}
645:                           <span className={cn(
646:                             "text-base font-bold mb-0.5 transition-colors",
647:                             isSelected && isActive ? "text-primary" : "text-foreground",
648:                             !isActive && "line-through decoration-destructive/30 decoration-1"
649:                           )}>
650:                             <div className="font-medium text-center">
651:                               {option.quantity}
652:                               {option.price > 0 && !allPricesSame && isActive && <span className="ml-1 text-xs text-primary font-bold">+₹{option.price}</span>}
653:                             </div>
654:                           </span>
655:                         </button>
656:                       );
657:                     });
658:                   })()}
659:                 </div>
660:               </div>
661:             )}
662:             {/* Colour Selector */}
663:             {product.colors && product.colors.length > 0 && (
664:               <div className="space-y-4 pt-4">
665:                 <div className="flex items-center justify-between pb-2 border-b border-border/30 mb-6">
666:                   <label className="text-xs font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-[0.15em]">Select Color</label>
667:                   <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-primary/60 bg-primary/5 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-primary/10">REQUIRED</span>
668:                 </div>
669:                 <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2">
670:                   {product.colors.map((colour) => {
671:                     const isActive = colour.colourStatus !== 'INACTIVE' && colour.colourStatus !== 'OUTOFSTOCK';
672:                     const statusLabel = colour.colourStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ? 'Sold Out' : (colour.colourStatus === 'INACTIVE' ? 'Unavailable' : undefined);
673: 
674:                     return (
675:                       <ColourCard
676:                         key={colour.id}
677:                         name={colour.name}
678:                         image={colour.image}
679:                         isSelected={selectedColourId === colour.id}
680:                         active={isActive}
681:                         statusLabel={statusLabel}
682:                         onClick={() => setSelectedColourId(colour.id)}
683:                       />
684:                     );
685:                   })}
686:                 </div>
687:               </div>
688:             )}
689: 
690:             {/* SizeColours (Select Colour) */}
691:             {availableSizeColours.length > 0 && (
692:               <div className="space-y-4 pt-4">
693:               <div className="flex items-center justify-between pb-2 border-b border-border/30 mb-6">
694:                   <label className="text-xs font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-[0.15em]">Select Style</label>
695:                   <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-primary/60 bg-primary/5 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-primary/10">REQUIRED</span>
696:                 </div>
697:                 <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-3">
698:                   {availableSizeColours.map(sc => {
699:                     const isSelected = selectedSizeColourId === sc.id;
700:                     const isActive = sc.sizeColourStatus !== 'INACTIVE' && sc.sizeColourStatus !== 'OUTOFSTOCK';
701: 
702:                     return (
703:                       <button
704:                         key={sc.id}
705:                         onClick={() => isActive && setSelectedSizeColourId(sc.id)}
706:                         className={cn(
707:                           "relative flex flex-col items-center p-1.5 rounded-xl border transition-all duration-300 h-[80px] sm:h-[90px]",
708:                           isSelected && isActive
709:                             ? "border-primary bg-primary/[0.03] shadow-md scale-[1.02]"
710:                             : isActive
711:                               ? "border-border/40 bg-secondary/10 hover:border-primary/20 hover:bg-secondary/20"
712:                               : "cursor-not-allowed bg-muted/10 border-border/20 opacity-50"
713:                         )}
714:                       >
715:                         {!isActive && (
716:                           <div className="absolute inset-0 z-20 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/5 rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
717:                             <div className="relative overflow-hidden px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-white/20 backdrop-blur-md border border-white/20 shadow-sm rotate-[-4deg]">
718:                               <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/10 to-transparent -translate-x-full animate-[shimmer_2s_infinite]" />
719:                               <span className="relative z-10 text-[8px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider text-rose-500 drop-shadow-sm">
720:                                 Sold Out
721:                               </span>
722:                             </div>
723:                           </div>
724:                         )}
725:                         {isSelected && isActive && (
726:                           <div className="absolute -top-2 -right-2 bg-primary text-primary-foreground rounded-full p-1 shadow-sm z-10">
727:                             <Check className="w-3 h-3" strokeWidth={3} />
728:                           </div>
729:                         )}
730:                         <div className="relative w-10 h-10 mb-1.5 rounded-full overflow-hidden border border-border/50 bg-white">
731:                           {sc.productPics ? (
732:                             <img src={sc.productPics} alt={sc.name} className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
733:                           ) : (
734:                             <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-bold text-muted-foreground/50">
735:                               {sc.name.charAt(0)}
736:                             </div>
737:                           )}
738:                         </div>
739:                         <span className={cn(
740:                           "text-xs font-bold tracking-tight line-clamp-1 w-full text-center px-1 mb-0.5 transition-colors",
741:                           isSelected && isActive ? "text-primary" : "text-foreground",
742:                           !isActive && "line-through decoration-destructive/30 decoration-1"
743:                         )}>
744:                           {sc.name}
745:                         </span>
746:                         {isActive && (
747:                           <span className={cn("text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wider leading-none", isSelected ? "text-primary/80" : "text-muted-foreground")}>
748:                             {sc.price > 0 ? `+₹${sc.price}` : "Standard"}
749:                           </span>
750:                         )}
751:                       </button>
