<content>
1: 'use client';
2: 
3: import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
4: import Image from 'next/image';
5: import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
6: import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react';
7: 
8: interface MediaItem {
9:     url: string;
10:     type: 'image' | 'video';
11: }
12: 
13: interface HeroCarouselProps {
14:     media: MediaItem[];
15:     autoPlayInterval?: number;
16: }
17: 
18: export function HeroCarousel({ media, autoPlayInterval = 6000 }: HeroCarouselProps) {
19:     const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0);
20:     const [isTransitioning, setIsTransitioning] = useState(false);
21: 
22:     const nextSlide = useCallback(() => {
23:         if (isTransitioning) return;
24:         setIsTransitioning(true);
25:         setCurrentIndex((prev) => (prev + 1) % media.length);
26:         setTimeout(() => setIsTransitioning(false), 1000);
27:     }, [media.length, isTransitioning]);
28: 
29:     const prevSlide = useCallback(() => {
30:         if (isTransitioning) return;
31:         setIsTransitioning(true);
32:         setCurrentIndex((prev) => (prev - 1 + media.length) % media.length);
33:         setTimeout(() => setIsTransitioning(false), 1000);
34:     }, [media.length, isTransitioning]);
35: 
36:     useEffect(() => {
37:         if (media.length <= 1) return;
38:         const interval = setInterval(nextSlide, autoPlayInterval);
39:         return () => clearInterval(interval);
40:     }, [nextSlide, autoPlayInterval, media.length]);
41: 
42:     if (!media || media.length === 0) return null;
43: 
44:     return (
45:         <div className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full overflow-hidden">
46:             {media.map((item, index) => (
47:                 <div
48:                     key={`${item.url}-${index}`}
49:                     className={cn(
50:                         "absolute inset-0 w-full h-full transition-all duration-1000 ease-in-out transform",
51:                         index === currentIndex 
52:                             ? "opacity-100 scale-105 z-10" 
53:                             : "opacity-0 scale-110 z-0"
54:                     )}
55:                 >
56:                     {item.type === 'video' ? (
57:                         <video
58:                             src={item.url}
59:                             autoPlay
60:                             muted
61:                             loop
62:                             playsInline
63:                             className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full object-cover object-center"
64:                         />
65:                     ) : (
66:                         <Image
67:                             src={item.url}
68:                             alt="Hero Banner"
69:                             fill
70:                             className="object-cover object-center"
71:                             priority={index === 0}
72:                         />
73:                     )}
74:                 </div>
75:             ))}
76: 
77:             {/* Navigation Dots */}
78:             {media.length > 1 && (
79:                 <div className="absolute bottom-8 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-20 flex gap-3">
80:                     {media.map((_, index) => (
81:                         <button
82:                             key={index}
83:                             onClick={() => setCurrentIndex(index)}
84:                             className={cn(
85:                                 "w-2 h-2 rounded-full transition-all duration-300",
86:                                 index === currentIndex 
87:                                     ? "bg-primary w-8" 
88:                                     : "bg-white/40 hover:bg-white/60"
89:                             )}
90:                             aria-label={`Go to slide ${index + 1}`}

92:                     ))}

99:                     <button
100:                         onClick={prevSlide}
101:                         className="p-2 rounded-full bg-black/20 backdrop-blur-md text-white border border-white/10 hover:bg-black/40 transition-colors"

108:                     >
109:                         <ChevronRight className="w-6 h-6" />

32:     const { categories, setCategories, isCategoryExpired, markCategoryAsFetched } = useProduct();

35:     const categoryShape = theme?.categoryFrame || 'circle';
36: 
37:     const getShapeClass = (shape: string) => {
38:         switch (shape) {
39:             case 'square': return 'rounded-xl';
40:             case 'squircle': return 'rounded-[2rem]';
41:             default: return 'rounded-full';
42:         }

55:             const storedRole = localStorage.getItem('userRole');
56:             setIsLoggedIn(storedLogin);
57:             setUserRole(storedRole);

68:         if (categoryPage) {
69:             const category = categories.find(c => c.id === categoryId);
70:             const urlSlug = category ? slugify(category.name) : categoryId;
71:             router.push(`/category/${urlSlug}`);
72:         } else {
73:             setSelectedCategory(categoryId);
74: 
75:             setTimeout(() => {

78:                     const yOffset = -80;

80:                     window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
81:                 }
82:             }, 100);

93:     const [isLoadingCategory, setIsLoadingCategory] = useState<Record<string, boolean>>({});
94:     const fetchingRef = useRef<Record<string, boolean>>({});
95:     const mountTime = useRef(Date.now());
96: 
97:     const loadCategoryData = useCallback(async (categoryId: string) => {
98:         if (!categoryId || categoryId === 'undefined' || categoryId === 'null') return;
99:         const currentCategories = useProduct.getState().categories;
100:         if (!currentCategories || currentCategories.length === 0) return;
101: 
102:         const category = currentCategories.find(c => c.id === categoryId);
103:         if (!category) return;
104: 
105:         const expired = isCategoryExpired(categoryId);
106:         const serverCat = initialCategories.find(ic => ic.id === categoryId);
107:         const hasServerCatalogs = serverCat && serverCat.catalogs.length > 0;
108:         const isPreLoaded = !!hasServerCatalogs;
109:         const state = useProduct.getState();
110:         const timestampExists = state.categoryTimestamps && !!state.categoryTimestamps[categoryId];
111:         const shouldSkipAsPreloaded = isPreLoaded && !timestampExists;
112: 
113:         const timeSinceMount = Date.now() - mountTime.current;
114:         const isFreshMount = timeSinceMount < 10000;
115: 
116:         if ((category.catalogs.length === 0 || expired) && !isLoadingCategory[categoryId] && !fetchingRef.current[categoryId] && !shouldSkipAsPreloaded) {
117:             if (isPreLoaded && isFreshMount) return;
118: 
119:             fetchingRef.current[categoryId] = true;
120:             setIsLoadingCategory(prev => ({ ...prev, [categoryId]: true }));
121:             try {
122:                 const fetchedCategory = await fetchProductsByCategoryAction(categoryId, companyDetails?.deliveryBetween);
123:                 if (fetchedCategory) {
124:                     setCategories(prev => prev.map(c => c.id === categoryId ? {
125:                         ...c,
126:                         ...fetchedCategory,
127:                         name: fetchedCategory.name || c.name,
128:                         categoryImage: fetchedCategory.categoryImage || c.categoryImage,
129:                         catalogs: fetchedCategory.catalogs
130:                     } : c));
131:                     markCategoryAsFetched(categoryId);
132:                     return fetchedCategory;
133:                 }
134:             } catch (error) {
135:                 console.error("Failed to load category", error);
136:             } finally {
137:                 fetchingRef.current[categoryId] = false;
138:                 setIsLoadingCategory(prev => ({ ...prev, [categoryId]: false }));
139:             }
140:         }
141:     }, [initialCategories, companyDetails?.deliveryBetween, isLoadingCategory, isCategoryExpired, markCategoryAsFetched, setCategories]);

143:     useEffect(() => {
144:         if (activeCategoryId) {

159: 
160:     const selectedCatalog = catalogs.find(c => c.id === selectedCatalogId);

163:     const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState("");

168:     const allCategoryProducts: ProductWithImage[] = useMemo(() => {

174:                     imageHint: image?.imageHint || 'product image',

180: 
181:     const allNewArrivals: ProductWithImage[] = useMemo(() => {

183:             .filter(p => {
184:                 const created = new Date(p.createdAt);
185:                 const now = new Date();
186:                 return (Math.abs(now.getTime() - created.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60)) <= 48;
187:             })
188:             .map(p => {
189:                 const image = imageMap.get(p.imageId);
190:                 return {
191:                     ...p,

194:                 }
195:             })
196:             .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.updatedAt).getTime() - new Date(a.updatedAt).getTime())
197:             : [];
198:     }, [activeCategory, imageMap]);
199:     const newArrivals = useMemo(() => allNewArrivals.slice(0, 5), [allNewArrivals]);
200: 
201:     const allFamousProducts: ProductWithImage[] = useMemo(() => {
202:         return activeCategory ? activeCategory.catalogs.flatMap(c => c.products)

216: 
217:     const baseProducts: ProductWithImage[] = useMemo(() => {

219:             return selectedCatalog.products.map(p => {

243:     useEffect(() => {

255:

260:             }
261:         };

263:         return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);

272:     // --- End First Category Product Grid Logic ---

className=\"flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4 w-full sm:w-auto pt-4\">\n              <Button onClick={() => router.push('/')} size=\"lg\" className=\"rounded-full px-8 gap-2 bg-accent text-navy-900 hover:bg-accent/90\">\n                <ArrowLeft size={16} /> Back to Home\n              </Button>\n              <Button variant=\"outline\" size=\"lg\" onClick={() => router.back()} className=\"rounded-full px-8 border-border/50\">\n                Go Back\n              </Button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          <Separator className=\"mb-12\" />\n\n          <div className=\"space-y-8\">\n            <div className=\"text-center\">\n              <h2 className=\"text-2xl font-headline font-bold mb-2\">Explore Popular Items</h2>\n              <p className=\"text-muted-foreground font-light\">You might find something else you love</p>\n            </div>\n            <Recommendations />\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    );\n  }\n\n  const currentPricingOption = product.pricing?.find(p => p.id === selectedPricingId) || (product.pricing?.[0]);\n  const availableSizeColours = currentPricingOption?.sizeColours || [];\n\n  const basePrice = currentPricingOption ? currentPricingOption.price : product.price;\n  const sizeColoursPrice = availableSizeColours\n    .filter(sc => sc.id === selectedSizeColourId)\n    .reduce((sum, sc) => sum + sc.price, 0);\n\n  let effectiveBasePrice = basePrice;\n  let originalPrice = basePrice;\n  let offerPercentage = 0;\n\n  const offerPercent = product.productOffer ? parseFloat(product.productOffer.toString().replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '')) : 0;\n\n  if (offerPercent > 0 && basePrice === product.price) {\n    const discountAmount = (basePrice * offerPercent) / 100;\n    effectiveBasePrice = Math.round(basePrice - discountAmount);\n    offerPercentage = offerPercent;\n  }\n  else if (currentPricingOption && currentPricingOption.priceAfterDiscount && currentPricingOption.priceAfterDiscount > 0) {\n    effectiveBasePrice = currentPricingOption.priceAfterDiscount;\n    originalPrice = currentPricingOption.price;\n    offerPercentage = Math.round(((originalPrice - effectiveBasePrice) / originalPrice) * 100);\n  }\n  else if (basePrice === product.price && product.priceAfterDiscount && product.priceAfterDiscount > 0) {\n    effectiveBasePrice = product.priceAfterDiscount;\n    originalPrice = product.price;\n    offerPercentage = Math.round(((originalPrice - effectiveBasePrice) / originalPrice) * 100);\n  }\n\n  const finalPrice = effectiveBasePrice + sizeColoursPrice;\n  const hasDiscount = effectiveBasePrice < originalPrice;\n\n  const handleAddToCart = () => {\n    const variantInfo = { ...selectedVariants };\n    if (currentPricingOption) {\n      variantInfo['Quantity'] = currentPricingOption.quantity;\n    }\n\n    const sizeColourObjects = availableSizeColours.filter(sc => sc.id === selectedSizeColourId);\n\n    const selectedColour = product.colors?.find(c => c.id === selectedColourId);\n    const colourToAdd = selectedColour ? {\n      id: selectedColour.id,\n      name: selectedColour.name,\n      image: selectedColour.image || ''\n    } : undefined;\n\n    const isOutOfStock = product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ||\n      (currentPricingOption?.sizeStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK') ||\n      (sizeColourObjects.some(sc => sc.sizeColourStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK')) ||\n      (selectedColour?.colourStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK');\n\n    if (isOutOfStock) {\n      toast({\n        title: \"Out of Stock\",\n        description: \"One of the selected options is currently unavailable.\",\n        variant: \"destructive\",\n      });\n      return;\n    }\n\n    addToCart(\n      { ...product, price: effectiveBasePrice, productSizeId: selectedPricingId || undefined },\n      variantInfo,\n      sizeColourObjects,\n      colourToAdd\n    );\n    setCartOpen(true);\n  };\n\n  const isWishlisted = isInWishlist(product.id);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"relative min-h-screen py-8\">\n      <div className=\"absolute inset-0 bg-dot-grid pointer-events-none\" />\n      <div className=\"absolute top-0 right-0 w-96 h-96 rounded-full bg-accent/3 blur-[120px] pointer-events-none\" />\n      <div className=\"absolute bottom-0 left-0 w-80 h-80 rounded-full bg-navy-800/5 blur-[100px] pointer-events-none\" />\n\n      <div className=\"container mx-auto px-4 relative z-10\">\n        <div className=\"mb-6\">\n          <Button variant=\"ghost\" onClick={() => router.back()} className=\"text-muted-foreground group hover:text-accent rounded-xl\">\n            <ArrowLeft className=\"h-5 w-5 mr-2 group-hover:-translate-x-1 transition-transform\" />\n            Back\n          </Button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-10 lg:gap-16\">\n          {/* Product Image Carousel */}\n          <div className=\"relative\">\n            <div className=\"relative aspect-[4/5] w-full rounded-3xl overflow-hidden bg-secondary/5 border border-border/30 shadow-xl card-3d\">\n              {(() => {\n                const imagesList: string[] = [];\n\n                const isDummyImage = (src: string) => {\n                  if (!src) return true;\n                  return src.includes('images.unsplash.com') && src.includes('w=800&q=80');\n                };\n\n                if (selectedSizeColourId) {\n                  const sc = availableSizeColours.find(sc => sc.id === selectedSizeColourId);\n                  if (sc && sc.productPics && sc.productPics.trim() !== \"\") imagesList.push(sc.productPics);\n                }\n\n                if (product.colors && product.colors.length > 0) {\n                  const selected = product.colors.find(c => c.id === selectedColourId);\n                  if (selected && selected.image && selected.image.trim() !== \"\" && !imagesList.includes(selected.image)) {\n                    imagesList.push(selected.image);\n                  }\n                }\n\n                const hasVariantImages = imagesList.length > 0;\n\n                if (product.images && product.images.length > 0) {\n                  product.images.forEach(img => {\n                    if (img && !imagesList.includes(img)) {\n                      if (!hasVariantImages || !isDummyImage(img)) {\n                        imagesList.push(img);\n                      }\n                    }\n                  });\n                } else if (product.productImage && !imagesList.includes(product.productImage)) {\n                  if (!hasVariantImages || !isDummyImage(product.productImage)) {\n                    imagesList.push(product.productImage);\n                  }\n                } else if (product.imageUrl && !imagesList.includes(product.imageUrl)) {\n                  if (!hasVariantImages) {\n                    imagesList.push(product.imageUrl);\n                  }\n                }\n\n                if (imagesList.length === 0) {\n                  imagesList.push(product.imageUrl || '');\n                }\n\n                return <ProductImageCarousel images={imagesList} alt={product.name} />\n              })()}\n\n              {(product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' || product.productStatus === 'INACTIVE') && (\n                <div className=\"absolute inset-0 z-20 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/5 backdrop-blur-[2px]\">\n                  <div className=\"relative overflow-hidden px-8 py-3 rounded-2xl bg-white/10 backdrop-blur-md border border-white/20 shadow-[0_8px_32px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)] transform rotate-[-5deg] animate-in zoom-in duration-500\">\n                    <span className={cn(\n                      \"relative z-10 text-xl font-black uppercase tracking-[0.2em] drop-shadow-sm\",\n                      product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ? \"text-rose-500\" : \"text-slate-400\"\n                    )}>\n                      {product.productStatus === 'OUTOFSTOCK' ? \"Sold Out\" : \"Unavailable\"}\n                    </span>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </div>\n\n            {/* Share / Wishlist floating buttons */}\n            <div className=\"absolute top-4 right-4 z-10 flex flex-col gap-2\">\n              <Button\n                variant=\"outline\"\n                size=\"icon\"\n                className=\"rounded-full h-10 w-10 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-md border-border/50 hover:bg-background shadow-lg\"\n                onClick={() => toggleWishlist(product)}\n              >\n                <Heart className={cn(\"h-4 w-4\", isWishlisted ? \"fill-red-500 text-red-500\" : \"\")} />\n              </Button>\n              <Button\n                variant=\"outline\"\n                size=\"icon\"\n                className=\"rounded-full h-10 w-10 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-md border-border/50 hover:bg-background shadow-lg\"\n              >\n                <Share2 className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n              </Button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Product Details */}\n          <div className=\"flex flex-col gap-6\">\n            <div>\n              <div className=\"space-y-1.5\">\n                <div className=\"inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1 rounded-full bg-accent/10 border border-accent/20 mb-3\">\n                  <span className=\"w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-accent animate-pulse-gold\" />\n                  <span className={cn(\n                    \"text-[9px] font-bold tracking-[0.2em] uppercase\",\n                    tenant.id.toLowerCase().includes('anantha') ? \"text-accent font-display tracking-[0.3em]\" : \"text-accent\"\n                  )}>\n                    {companyDetails?.companyName || 'Tirumala           </div>\n\n              <div className=\"flex items-baseline gap-3 mt-6\">\n                <h2 className=\"text-3xl md:text-4xl font-headline font-bold text-accent tracking-tight\">\n                  ₹{(finalPrice).toFixed(2)}\n                </h2>\n                {hasDiscount && (\n                  <span className=\"text-base text-muted-foreground/60 line-through decoration-destructive/30 decoration-1\">\n                    ₹{(originalPrice + sizeColoursPrice).toFixed(2)}\n                  </span>\n                )}\n                {hasDiscount && (\n                  <span className=\"text-xs font-bold text-white bg-gradient-to-r from-emerald-500 to-emerald-400 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full shadow-lg animate-in zoom-in ml-2\">\n                    {offerPercentage}% OFF\n                  </span>\n                )}\n              </div>\n\n              <p className=\"text-[11px] font-medium text-muted-foreground/60 mt-2 flex items-center ₹${companyDetails.freeDeliveryCost}`}\n              </p>\n\n              {/* Rating */}\n              <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3 mt-4\">\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1\">\n                  {(() => {\n                    const pid = Number(product.id) || product.id.toString().charCodeAt(0);\n                    const randomRating = 4.1 + (pid % 6) * 0.1;\n                    return [...Array(5)].map((_, i) => (\n                      <Star key={i} className={cn(\"h-4 w-4\", i < Math.floor(randomRating) ? className=\"text-muted-foreground text-sm font-medium\">\n                  ({(() => {\n                    const pid = Number(product.id) || product.id.toString().charCodeAt(0);\n                    return (4.1 + (pid % 6) * 0.1).toFixed(1);\n                  })()})\n                </span>\n                <span className=\"text-muted-foreground/40 text-sm\">|</span>\n                <span className=\"text-muted-foreground text-sm\">{(product.reviews?.length || 0) + Math.floor(Math.random() * 50)} reviews</span>\n              </div>\n\n              <p className=\"mt-6     </div>\n                )}\n              </div>\n            )}\n\n            {product.instructions && (\n              <div className=\"rounded-2xl p-5 border border-border/30        {/* Pricing Options */}\n              {product.pricing && product.pricing.length > 0 && (\n                <div className=\"space-y-4\">\n                  <div className=\"flex items-center         <span className=\"text-[9px] font-bold text-accent bg-accent/10 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-accent/20\">REQUIRED</span>\n                  </div>\n                  <div               setSelectedSizeColourId(null);\n                              }\n                            }}\n                            className={cn(\n                              \"relative flex  >\n                            {!isActive && (\n                              <div className=\"absolute inset-0 z-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/5 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden\">\n       <span className=\"relative z-10 text-[8px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider text-rose-500 drop-shadow-sm\">\n                                    Sold Out\n       <div className=\"absolute top-2 right-2 text-accent\">\n                                <svg className=\"w-4 h-4\" fill=\"none\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\" stroke=\"currentColor\"><path                     !isActive && \"line-through decoration-destructive/30 decoration-1\"\n                            )}>\n                              <div className=\"font-medium text-center\">\n                                {option.quantity}\n                                {option.price > 0 && !allPricesSame && isActive && <span className=\"ml-1 text-xs text-accent });\n                    })()}\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              )}\n\n              {/* Colour Selector */}\n              {product.colors && product.colors.length > 0 371:                       <Sparkles className="w-3 h-3 text-yellow-300 fill-yellow-300 animate-pulse" />
372:                       <div className="flex flex-col leading-none items-start">
373:                         <span className="text-[8px] opacity-90 font-medium uppercase tracking-wider">Buy &gt; {threshold}</span>
374:                         <span className="text-[10px] font-extrabold">Get {discount}% Off</span>
375:                       </div>
376:                     </div>
377:                   );
378:                 }
379:               }
380:               return null;
381:             })()}
382:           </div>
383: 
384:           {/* Wishlist Button */}
385:           <Button
386:             variant="ghost"
387:             size="icon"
388:             className="absolute top-3 right-3 h-8 w-8 rounded-full bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-md hover:bg-background text-muted-foreground transition-all duration-300 shadow-sm z-20"
389:             onClick={handleWishlistClick}
390:           >
391:             <Heart
392:               className={cn(
393:                 "w-4 h-4 transition-colors",
394:                 isWishlisted ? "fill-primary text-primary" : "text-muted-foreground"
395:               )}
396:             />
397:           </Button>
398: 
399:           {/* Quick Add Overlay - Desktop Only - Hide if Disabled */}
400:           {!isDisabled && (
401:             <div className="absolute inset-x-0 bottom-0 p-3 transition-transform duration-500 ease-out z-20 translate-y-full group-hover:translate-y-0 hidden md:block">
402:               <div onClick={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); }}>
403:                 <AddToCartSheet product={product}>
404:                   <Button className="w-full rounded-full shadow-lg shadow-primary/25 font-semibold h-10 text-sm transition-all hover:shadow-primary/40">
405:                     {text.quickAddButton || "Quick Add"}
406:                   </Button>
407:                 </AddToCartSheet>
408:               </div>
409:             </div>
410:           )}
411:         </div>
412: 
413:         {/* Content - Compact Spacing */}
414:         <CardContent className="p-4 flex flex-col gap-2 flex-1">
415:           {/* Header Row */}
416:           <div className="flex justify-between items-start gap-2 min-h-[3.5rem]">
417:             <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
418:               <h3 className={cn(
419:                 "font-bold text-sm md:text-base text-foreground leading-tight overflow-hidden",
420:                 useTenant().id.toLowerCase().includes('anantha') ? "font-display uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-[11px]" : "font-headline line-clamp-2"
421:               )} title={product.name}>
422:                 {product.name}
423:               </h3>
424:             </div>
425:             <div className="flex flex-col items-end shrink-0 pt-0.5">
426:               {(() => {
427:                 let displayPrice = 0;
428:                 let originalPriceForDisplay = 0;
429:                 let hasDiscount = false;
430:                 let showStartsFrom = false;
431: 
432:                 if (product.price && product.price > 0) {
433:                   const offerPercent = product.productOffer ? parseFloat(product.productOffer.toString().replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '')) : 0;
434: 
435:                   if (offerPercent > 0) {
436:                     const discountAmount = (product.price * offerPercent) / 100;
437:                     displayPrice = Math.round(product.price - discountAmount);
438:                     originalPriceForDisplay = product.price;
439:                     hasDiscount = true;
440:                   } else {
441:                     const offerPrice = (product as any).priceAfterDiscount;
442:                     if (offerPrice && offerPrice < product.price) {
443:                       displayPrice = offerPrice;
444:                       originalPriceForDisplay = product.price;
445:                       hasDiscount = true;
446:                     } else {
447:                       displayPrice = product.price;
448:                     }
449:                   }
450:                 } else if (product.pricing && product.pricing.length > 0) {
451:                   showStartsFrom = true;
452:                   let minP = Infinity;
453:                   product.pricing.forEach(p => {
454:                     const final = (p.priceAfterDiscount && p.priceAfterDiscount > 0) ? p.priceAfterDiscount : p.price;
455:                     if (final < minP) minP = final;
456:                   });
457:                   displayPrice = minP;
458:                 }
459: 
460:                 return (
461:                   <span className="font-headline font-bold text-base text-primary tracking-tight text-right">
462:                     <span className="flex flex-col items-end">
463:                       {showStartsFrom && <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground font-medium uppercase tracking-wider leading-none mb-0.5">Starts from</span>}
464:                       <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 justify-end">
465:                         {hasDiscount && (
466:                           <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground line-through font-medium">₹{originalPriceForDisplay}</span>
467:                         )}
468:                         <span className="leading-none">₹{displayPrice}</span>
469:                       </div>

(Showing lines 270-469 of 568. Use offset=470 to continue.)
</content>
```
